<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports items, labels, groups of items</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Focus is fully managed using <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">aria-activedescendant</code> pattern</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Typeahead to allow focusing items by typing text</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Keyboard navigation support including arrow keys, home/end, page up/down</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anatomy" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Anatomy<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Check the menu anatomy and part names.</p>

<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute to help identify them in the DOM.</p>

<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the menu package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> menu</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/menu&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The menu package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - Behavior logic for the menu.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps behavior to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Pass a unique <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">useMachine</code> so generated element ids stay predictable.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>
<p>To show the menu when a trigger element is right-clicked, use
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.getContextTriggerProps()</code>.</p>
<p>Context menus also open during a long-press of roughly <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">700ms</code> when the pointer
is pen or touch.</p>

<h3 id="default-open-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Default open state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#default-open-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultOpen</code> for an uncontrolled initial state.</p>

<h3 id="controlling-open-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlling open state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlling-open-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onOpenChange</code> to control the open state.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>menu<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h3 id="listening-for-highlighted-items" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for highlighted items<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-highlighted-items"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onHighlightChange</code> to react when keyboard or pointer highlight changes.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>menu<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">highlightedValue</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-item-selection" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for item selection<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-item-selection"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onSelect</code> to react when an item is selected.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>menu<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onSelect</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { value: string }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="positioning-the-menu" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Positioning the menu<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#positioning-the-menu"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">positioning</code> to configure menu placement.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>menu<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">positioning</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">placement</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;right-start&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="keeping-the-menu-open-after-selection" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Keeping the menu open after selection<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#keeping-the-menu-open-after-selection"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnSelect</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">false</code> to keep the menu open after selecting an item.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>menu<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">closeOnSelect</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each menu part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<h3 id="highlighted-item-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Highlighted item state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#highlighted-item-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When an item is highlighted, via keyboard navigation or pointer, it is given a
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-highlighted</code> attribute.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-highlighted</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for highlighted state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-type</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;radio|checkbox&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-highlighted</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for highlighted state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disabled-item-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabled item state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabled-item-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When an item or an option item is disabled, it is given a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-disabled</code>
attribute.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for disabled state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-type</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;radio|checkbox&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for disabled state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="using-arrows" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Using arrows<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#using-arrows"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When using arrows within the menu, you can style it using CSS variables.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;arrow&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token variable">--arrow-background</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token color">red</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="checked-option-item-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Checked option item state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#checked-option-item-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When an option item is checked, it is given a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-state</code> attribute.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-type</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;radio|checkbox&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;checked&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for checked state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The menu machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ trigger: string; contextTrigger: string; content: string; groupLabel: (id: string) =&gt; string; group: (id: string) =&gt; string; positioner: string; arrow: string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the menu. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultHighlightedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The initial highlighted value of the menu item when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the highlighted value of the menu item.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">highlightedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The controlled highlighted value of the menu item.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onHighlightChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: HighlightChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the highlighted menu item changes.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onSelect</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: SelectionDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when a menu item is selected.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">anchorPoint</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Point</code><span class="d_block">The positioning point for the menu. Can be set by the context menu trigger or the button trigger.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">loopFocus</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to loop the keyboard navigation.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">positioning</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">PositioningOptions</code><span class="d_block">The options used to dynamically position the menu</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnSelect</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to close the menu when an option is selected</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">aria-label</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The accessibility label for the menu</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">The controlled open state of the menu</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onOpenChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: OpenChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the menu opens or closes</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultOpen</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">The initial open state of the menu when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the open state of the menu.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">typeahead</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the pressing printable characters should trigger typeahead navigation</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">composite</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the menu is a composed with other composite widgets like a combobox or tabs</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">navigate</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: NavigateDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to navigate to the selected item if it&#x27;s an anchor element</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;ltr&quot; | &quot;rtl&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The document&#x27;s text/writing direction.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The unique identifier of the machine.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getRootNode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; ShadowRoot | Node | Document</code><span class="d_block">A root node to correctly resolve document in custom environments. E.x.: Iframes, Electron.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onEscapeKeyDown</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: KeyboardEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the escape key is pressed</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onRequestDismiss</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: LayerDismissEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when this layer is closed due to a parent layer being closed</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onPointerDownOutside</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: PointerDownOutsideEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the pointer is pressed down outside the component</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onFocusOutside</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: FocusOutsideEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the focus is moved outside the component</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onInteractOutside</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: InteractOutsideEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when an interaction happens outside the component</span></li></ul>

<h2 id="accessibility" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Accessibility<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Uses
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/menu-button/examples/menu-button-actions-active-descendant/" class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px">aria-activedescendant</a>
pattern to manage focus movement among menu items.</p>
<h3 id="keyboard-interactions" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Keyboard Interactions<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#keyboard-interactions"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>

fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Enter</kbd></div><div>Activates/Selects the highlighted item</div></li><li class="d_flex bdr_3px">ArrowUp</kbd></div><div>Highlights the previous item in the menu</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd likely forgot to import, pass, or provide it.\")}"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"12:T110a,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"An accessible dropdown and context menu that is used to display a list of\nactions or options that a user can choose when a trigger element is\nright-clicked or long pressed.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/menu\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"ContextMenu\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Supports items, labels, groups of items\n- Focus is fully managed using `aria-activedescendant` pattern\n- Typeahead to allow focusing items by typing text\n- Keyboard navigation support including arrow keys, home/end, page up/down\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the menu package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"menu/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nCheck the menu anatomy and part names.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"menu\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the menu package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as menu from \"@zag-js/menu\"\n```\n\nThe menu package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - Behavior logic for the menu.\n- `connect` - Maps behavior to JSX props and event handlers.\n\n\u003e Pass a unique `id` to `useMachine` so generated element ids stay predictable.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\nTo show the menu when a trigger element is right-clicked, use\n`api.getContextTriggerProps()`.\n\nContext menus also open during a long-press of roughly `700ms` when the pointer\nis pen or touch.\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"menu/context-menu.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Default open state\n\nUse `defaultOpen` for an uncontrolled initial state.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(menu.machine, {\n  defaultOpen: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Controlling open state\n\nUse `open` and `onOpenChange` to control the open state.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(menu.machine, {\n  open,\n  onOpenChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { open: boolean }\n    setOpen(details.open)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for highlighted items\n\nUse `onHighlightChange` to react when keyboard or pointer highlight changes.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(menu.machine, {\n  onHighlightChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { highlightedValue: string | null }\n    console.log(details.highlightedValue)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for item selection\n\nUse `onSelect` to react when an item is selected.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(menu.machine, {\n  onSelect(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string }\n    console.log(details.value)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Positioning the menu\n\nUse `positioning` to configure menu placement.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(menu.machine, {\n  positioning: { placement: \"right-start\" },\n})\n```\n\n### Keeping the menu open after selection\n\nSet `closeOnSelect` to `false` to keep the menu open after selecting an item.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(menu.machine, {\n  closeOnSelect: false,\n})\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach menu part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n### Highlighted item state\n\nWhen an item is highlighted, via keyboard navigation or pointer, it is given a\n`data-highlighted` attribute.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"item\"][data-highlighted] {\n  /* styles for highlighted state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"item\"][data-type=\"radio|checkbox\"][data-highlighted] {\n  /* styles for highlighted state */\n}\n```\n\n### Disabled item state\n\nWhen an item or an option item is disabled, it is given a `data-disabled`\nattribute.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"item\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"item\"][data-type=\"radio|checkbox\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for disabled state */\n}\n```\n\n### Using arrows\n\nWhen using arrows within the menu, you can style it using CSS variables.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"arrow\"] {\n  --arrow-size: 20px;\n  --arrow-background: red;\n}\n```\n\n### Checked option item state\n\nWhen an option item is checked, it is given a `data-state` attribute.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"item\"][data-type=\"radio|checkbox\"][data-state=\"checked\"] {\n  /* styles for checked state */\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe menu machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"menu\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe menu `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"menu\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"menu\" /\u003e\n\n### CSS Variables\n\n\u003cCssVarTable name=\"menu\" /\u003e\n\n## Accessibility\n\nUses\n[aria-activedescendant](https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/menu-button/examples/menu-button-actions-active-descendant/)\npattern to manage focus movement among menu items.\n\n### Keyboard Interactions\n\n\u003cKeyboardTable name=\"context-menu\" /\u003e"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Context
